<span data-ttu-id="9a55f-1708">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2008 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9a55f-1708">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008 R2:</span></span>
